msg:Objectively speaking, the reasons for the bad reviews
1. The hotel hosted the CPPCC meeting, and it is understandable that ordinary people check in at the corner through the side door. After many twists and turns, we walked to the employee passage, shared three elevators with the sanitary vehicles and maintenance items, and were not informed after the meeting was over
2. I took the normal guest elevator to the room by myself, and the room card could not be swiped at all
3. I went to the front desk to handle it, and I had to wait for the previous guests to check in. It was really uncomfortable to stand with a low fever. It could be handled in a dozen seconds, but I had to wait for half a day. Then when I asked for the parking ticket, the front desk asked me for the car number. The original words were: "You tell me", is this the service language of a five-star hotel?
4. The air conditioner must be at 26 degrees. If it is lower, it will blow out cold wind, which makes it very hot all night
5. Maybe they are afraid that the guests will be unhappy to take the employee elevator, so they said that they upgraded the room. I think it may be a little high. This is the so-called "garden view room", yes, the "construction site view room" that has not been completed yet
